<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">belastinge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">burden, accusation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belasting.html>belasting</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tax</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">money</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belastinggeld.html>belastinggeld</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belastinggelden.html>belastinggelden</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tax money</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Very commonly used as a political spin term for “public money” or “government money”, which would be <i><a href = vnd.unilang:publiek.html>publiek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overheidsgeld.html>overheidsgeld</a></i> respectively. This usage <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered incorrect by economists.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:belastinggeld.html>belastinggeld</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belastingbetaler.html>belastingbetaler</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> staatskas <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ingebracht.html>ingebracht</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevolg.html>gevolg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:problemen.html>problemen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:automatisering.html>automatisering</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> in Nederland <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schatting.html>schatting</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaarlijks.html>jaarlijks</a> één <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijf.html>vijf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:miljard.html>miljard</a> euro <b><a href = vnd.unilang:belastinggeld.html>belastinggeld</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weggegooid.html>weggegooid</a>. <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***belediging.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:belediging.html>belediging</a> (6098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beledigen.html>beledigen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to insult</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ing, -ation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belediging.html>belediging</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beledigingen.html>beledigingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belediging.html>beledigingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>insult, verbal abuse
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">beschimping</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***beleefd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beleefd.html>beleefd</a> (3105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beleefd.html>beleefd</a></i>, in the older sense "to observe (a custom)". The word, itself a conjugation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beleven.html>beleven</a></i>, thus originally meant "observing custom or protocol".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beleefd.html>beleefd</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beleefd.html>beleefder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">beleefdst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>polite (well-mannered)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beleggen.html>beleggen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leggen.html>leggen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beleggen.html>beleggen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover, smear, butter, spread <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> (e.g. a piece of bread with butter and jam)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to invest money</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to convoke, to call a meeting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to belay, to fasten (a rope), to fasten (with rope)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover with</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plan, to devise</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:belegger.html>belegger</a> (71018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beleggen.html>beleggen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to invest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belezen.html>belezen</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belezen.html>belezener</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">belezenst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>well-read, well informed and knowledgeable because of extensive reading</li>
<li>hence book-smart, erudite</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:belladonna.html>belladonna</a> (45840)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:belladonna.html>belladonna</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos"><i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = lady</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, altered by <span class="Latn" lang="en">folk etymology</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">blādōna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nightshade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">*blātōnā</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">blātunā</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*blātus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span ***bellen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a> (431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bel.html>bel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a>, like using a bell</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call, by bell (originally) or (now mostly) telephone; to dial</li></ol>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opbellen.html>opbellen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bellan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bellaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bellow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">блеять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blejatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:baa.html>baa</a>, bleat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***bellows.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a> (61699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">belwes</i>, plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">belu</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">belw</i>, a northern form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">beli</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:belg.html>belg</a></i>, cf. <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bælġ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*balgiz</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Balg</i>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">belly</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A device for delivering pressurized air in a controlled quantity to a controlled location. At its most simple <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a container which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> deformable in such a way as to alter its volume which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an outlet or outlets where one wishes to blow air.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">When wood fires <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> common, so <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a></b> for helping start them.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_C._Lincoln" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph C. Lincoln">Joseph C. Lincoln</a>,  chapter 8, in  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5535161W"><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Pratt's Patients</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">That <a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a wonder in its way. The handles that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> on it first <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> wore out long ago, and he'd made new <a href = vnd.unilang:ones.html>ones</a> of braided rope yarn. And the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> patched in more <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> than a cranberry <a href = vnd.unilang:picker.html>picker</a>'s <a href = vnd.unilang:overalls.html>overalls</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Any flexible container or enclosure, as one used to cover a moving joint.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal or archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The lungs.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">photography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Flexible, light-tight enclosures connecting the lensboard and the <a href = vnd.unilang:camera.html>camera</a> back.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> That which <a href = vnd.unilang:fans.html>fans</a> the fire of hatred, jealousy, etc.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>"<a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>Bellows</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used with both singular and plural verbs. One can <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> find "A <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>".</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">belly</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">blow</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">bellowses</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bellowsing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bellowsed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To operate a <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a>; to direct air at (something) using a <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a>.
<ul><li><b>1861</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Expectations" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Great Expectations">Great <a href = vnd.unilang:expectations.html>Expectations</a></a></i>, Chapter ,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/files/1400/1400-h/1400-h.htm">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> recommended to the place as a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> who could give another <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> as good as he <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a>, and I <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> it. It’s easier than <b>bellowsing</b> and hammering.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1915</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_G._Neihardt" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John G. Neihardt">John G. Neihardt</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cycle_of_the_West" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Cycle of the West">The Song of Hugh Glass</a></i>, New York: Macmillan, Part 2, p. 34,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/hughglasssongof00neihrich">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>So <b>bellowsed</b>, all the kindled soul of Hugh</dd>
<dd>Became a still white hell of brooding ire,</dd>
<dd>And through his <a href = vnd.unilang:veins.html>veins</a> regenerating fire</dd>
<dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ran.html>Ran</a>, driving out the lethargy of pain.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1920</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arthur_Guiterman" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Arthur Guiterman">Arthur Guiterman</a>, “Thunder-Storm” in <i>Ballads of Old New York</i>, New York: Harper amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:bros.html>Bros</a>., p. 49,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/cu31924022457752">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:smiths.html>smiths</a> of the heavens are mending the weather;</dd>
<dd>Their hammers are beating the fragments together.</dd>
<dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:cumulus.html>cumulus</a> mountains with nebulous gorges</dd>
<dd>Are dazzled with flame of the wind-<b>bellowsed</b> forges;</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1966</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anthony_Burgess" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Anthony Burgess">Anthony Burgess</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tremor_of_Intent:_An_Eschatological_Spy_Novel" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tremor of Intent: An Eschatological Spy Novel">Tremor of Intent: An Eschatological Spy Novel</a></i>, New York: Norton, Part 3, Chapter 6, p. 173,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/tremorofintent00burg">[4]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>He almost let the cigar go out. ‘Good <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>, no. <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>’re both exiles, <a href = vnd.unilang:aren.html>aren</a>’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>?’ He <b>bellowsed</b> the end red again and continued, delicate as a musician, his scoring.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1999</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ferdinand_Mount" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ferdinand Mount">Ferdinand Mount</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jem.html>Jem</a> (and <a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a>)</i>, New York: Carroll amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:graf.html>Graf</a>, Chapter 10, p. 397,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/jemandsamnovel00moun">[5]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a capricious devil, the furnace, though I say it myself, and it wants regular <b>bellowsing</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To expand and contract like a <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a>.
<ul><li><b>1904</b>, A. <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Sennett, <i>Across the Great Saint <a href = vnd.unilang:bernard.html>Bernard</a>: The Modes of Nature and the Manners of <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></i>, London: Bemrose amp; Sons, Chapter 6, p. 389,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/acrossgreatsain01senngoog">[6]</a></sup>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> [the dogs] sprang up, and, with a grand spraying of the crisp snow as they fleetly clambered up the steep side, they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> with us in an incredibly short time, with pink tongues protruding, sides <b>bellowsing</b>, and <a href = vnd.unilang:sterns.html>sterns</a> wagging.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1933</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Steinbeck" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Steinbeck">John Steinbeck</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Red_Pony" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Red Pony">The Red <a href = vnd.unilang:pony.html>Pony</a></a></i>, New York: Viking, 1945, Chapter 1, p. 48,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/redponystei00stei">[7]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>The <a href = vnd.unilang:pony.html>pony</a> still lay on his side and the wound in his throat <b>bellowsed</b> in and out.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1978</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_King" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Stephen King">Stephen King</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Stand" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Stand">The Stand</a></i>, New York: Random House, 2012, Chapter 25, p. 196,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=1xhLQ7F1_CsCamp;printsec=frontcoverv=onepageamp;qamp;f=false">[8]</a></sup>

***belust.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:belust.html>belust</a> (65935)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lust.html>lust</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belust.html>belust</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>eager, desiring [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(for, to)</span></span>] <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onverbiddelijk.html>Onverbiddelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genadeloos.html>genadeloos</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stapten.html>stapten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eenden.html>eenden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nader.html>nader</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:belust.html>belust</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Unrelenting and mercilessly the ducks stepped <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a>, deeply <b>craving for</b> bread.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Instead of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i> can be used when the argument <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an infinitive.</li>
<li>In older texts the prepositions <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a></i> or a complement genitive may be used in the same meaning as the preposition <i><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in modern language. These old usages are now obsolete.</li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geldbelust.html>geldbelust</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">machtsbelust</span></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bemachtigen.html>bemachtigen</a></i>.
